#SHX annexing by CHI
country_event = {
	id = kmt.1
	title = kmt.1.t
	desc = kmt.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 608 size > 10 }
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 614 size > 10 }
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 607 size > 5 }
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 796 size > 5 }
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 611 size > 10 }
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = PRC
				factor = -100
			}
		}
		name = kmt.1.a
		FROM = {
			annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
			country_event = { id = kmt.2 }
			set_country_flag = shx_sumitted
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Yen Hsi-shan"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					retire_country_leader = yes
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		name = kmt.1.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = kmt.3 days = 1 } }
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 70 }
		name = kmt.1.c
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
						create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
					type = annex_everything
					target = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					is_puppet_of = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = kmt.4 days = 1 } }
		FROM = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SHX modifier = KMT_SHX_refused } }
		SHX = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = SHX_SHX_refused } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = refused_shx_offer
		}
	}
}

#declare internal war propaganda lost
country_event = {
	id = kmt.6
	title = kmt.6.t
	desc = kmt.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest

	trigger = {
		has_idea = KMT_propaganda
		any_country = {
			is_chinese_nations = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_propaganda
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_propaganda_busted
				days = 600
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_propaganda
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_propaganda_busted
				days = 600
			}
		}
	}
}

			base = 5
		}
		name = kmt.11.a

			transfer_state = 434

		}
		add_political_power = -125
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		name = kmt.11.b
		trigger = {
			is_subject = yes
		}
		OVERLORD = { country_event = { id = kmt.11 days = 1 } }
		add_political_power = -500
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				CHI = { is_major = no }
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				CHI = { is_major = yes }
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = no
				CHI = { is_major = yes }
				factor = 0
			}

#redraw mcmahon - refused
country_event = {
	id = kmt.14
	title = kmt.14.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	desc = kmt.14.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = { has_war = no }
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = FROM
							ratio < 1
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { has_war = yes }
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = FROM
							ratio < 0.8
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		name = kmt.14.a
		add_political_power = -250
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_war = no
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = FROM
							ratio > 1.5
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_war = yes
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = FROM
							ratio > 2
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_war = no
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = FROM
							ratio > 2
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_war = yes
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = FROM
							ratio > 2.5
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				surrender_progress > 0.5
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = kmt.14.b
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = take_state_focus
			generator = { 434 }
		}
	}
}

#demand taiwan
country_event = {
	id = kmt.15
	title = kmt.15.t
	desc = {
		text = kmt.15.d_1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = SPR
				original_tag = HOL
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.15.d_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = SPR
				original_tag = HOL
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes


	#return - japan
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				FROM = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20

					target = FROM

				}
			}
		}

				}
				factor = 2
			}

				factor = 0.1

				}
			}
		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {

			base = 50

#taiwan refused
country_event = {
	id = kmt.17
	title = kmt.17.t
	desc = kmt.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.17.a
				create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
			type = take_state_focus
			target = FROM
			generator = { 524 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					ROOT = {
						is_faction_leader = no
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							ROOT = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					remove_from_faction = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#CHI wants to join allied
country_event = {
	id = kmt.21
	title = kmt.21.t
	desc = kmt.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.21.a
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			create_faction = Allies
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.22 }
			set_country_flag = KMT_eng_accepts_chi_into_faction
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.21.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = CHI_join_britain_rejected
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.23 }
		}
	}
}

#baihua stage 1
country_event = {
	id = kmt.33
	title = kmt.33.t
	desc = kmt.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = KMT_hundred_flowers_campaign }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = PRC_Hundred_Flowers_Campaign }
		OR = {
		focus_progress = {
			focus = KMT_hundred_flowers_campaign
			progress > 0.20
		}
		focus_progress = {
			focus = PRC_Hundred_Flowers_Campaign
			progress > 0.20
		}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
				}
				set_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		name = kmt.33.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = baihua_end_now
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_baihua_stage_1_finished
			days = 365
		}
		set_country_flag = baihua_completed
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		name = kmt.33.b
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = KMT_baihua_stage_1_idea
			add_idea = KMT_baihua_stage_2_idea
		}
	}
}

#baihua stage 2
country_event = {
	id = kmt.34
	title = kmt.34.t
	desc = kmt.34.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		#NOT = { has_completed_focus = PRC_hundred_flowers_campaign }
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = KMT_hundred_flowers_campaign }
		OR = {
		focus_progress = {
			focus = KMT_hundred_flowers_campaign
			progress > 0.40
		}
		#focus_progress = {
		#	focus = PRC_Hundred_Flowers_Campaign
		#	progress > 0.40
		#}					
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core }
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
				}
				set_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core }
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
				}
				set_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core }
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
				}
				set_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		name = kmt.34.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = baihua_end_now
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_baihua_stage_2_finished
			days = 365
		}
		add_ideas = KMT_baihua_stage_2_finished_effect
		set_country_flag = baihua_completed
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = PRC_baihua_core
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		name = kmt.34.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_baihua_stage_2_tt
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = KMT_baihua_stage_2_idea
			add_idea = KMT_baihua_stage_3_idea
		}
	}

#great leap furnace auto build
country_event = {
	id = kmt.40
	title = kmt.40.t
	desc = kmt.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_burma_road

	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_flag = KMT_great_leap_started
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 50
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
					}
				}
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 1
				}
				save_event_target_as = shitty_furnace_state
			}
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = kmt.40.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			event_target:shitty_furnace_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:shitty_furnace_state = {
				set_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
			}
		}
	}
}



country_event = {
	id = kmt.41
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_flag = KMT_great_leap_started
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
						is_owned_by = PRC
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
					is_owned_by = PRC
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced
		}
	}

	option = {}
}






#famine
country_event = {
	id = kmt.43
	title = kmt.43.t
	desc = kmt.43.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 73
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
		}
		has_country_flag = commune_visited
		tag = PRC
		any_state = {
			has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
				}
				add_manpower = -100000
				set_state_flag = KMT_great_leap_famine
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
						has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
					}
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.43.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = KMT_great_leap_famine
				}
				add_manpower = -100000
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
					has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
				}
			}
			add_ideas = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.44 }
		}
	}
}

#remove famine flag

		}
	}

#join comitern
country_event = {
	id = kmt.49
	title = kmt.49.t
	desc = kmt.49.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_02

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.49.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Leon Trotsky"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							has_completed_focus = KMT_kill_mao
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Leon Trotsky"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_global_flag = KMT_PRC_agrees_to_work_with_us
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.476 }
			set_country_flag = KMT_sov_accepts_chi_into_faction
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.49.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = SOV_CHI_join_comintern_reject
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.477 }
		}
	}
}

#demand events main central steppe
country_event = {
	id = kmt.52
	title = kmt.52.t
	desc = kmt.52.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			set_country_flag = kmt_52_fired
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					is_major = yes
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						OVERLORD = {
							is_major = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				all_owned_state = {
					all_neighbor_state = {
						NOT = {
							owner = { tag = FROM }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.52.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							region = 152
							region = 145
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					any_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							region = 152
							region = 145
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kmt.580 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_from_owned_steppe_states_tt2
				hidden_effect = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								region = 152
								region = 145
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							transfer_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_state = {
								NOT = {
									region = 145
									region = 152
								}
								is_owned_by = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
				}
				FROM = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.53 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.5
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.52.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
						create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = kmt.54 } } }
	}
}

#demand rejected
country_event = {
	id = kmt.54
	title = kmt.54.t
	desc = kmt.54.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.54.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = FROM
					is_subject_of = FROM
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						region = 152
						region = 145
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {

	title = kmt.56.t
	desc = kmt.56.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			set_country_flag = kmt_56_fired
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					is_major = yes
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						OVERLORD = {
							is_major = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						tag = ROOT
					}
					all_owned_state = {
						all_neighbor_state = {
							NOT = {
								owner = { tag = FROM }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.56.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 670
					owns_state = 671
					owns_state = 286
					owns_state = 741
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					OR = {
						owns_state = 670
						owns_state = 671
						owns_state = 286
						owns_state = 741
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kmt.580 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_from_owned_indochina_states_tt2
				hidden_effect = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 670
								state = 671
								state = 286
								state = 741
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							transfer_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_state = {
								NOT = {
									state = 670
									state = 671
									state = 286
									state = 741
								}
								is_owned_by = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
				}
				FROM = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.57 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.5
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.56.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
						create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = kmt.58 } } }
	}
}

#Surrender when china has taken all asia land
country_event = {
	id = kmt.64
	title = kmt.64.t
	desc = kmt.64.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_nationalist_china_machinegun_firing

	trigger = {
		always = no
		OR = {
			owns_state = 671
			owns_state = 670
			owns_state = 286
			owns_state = 741
		}
		any_country = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 2 }
		}
		check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 }
		NOT = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					state = 671
					state = 670
					state = 286
					state = 741
				}
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		all_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				state = 671
				state = 670
				state = 286
				state = 741
			}
			CONTROLLER = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 2 } }
		}
		has_civil_war = no
		is_in_faction = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }

	#Surrender and offer territory
	option = {
		name = kmt.64.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 65
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
				has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.65 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = kmt.64.a_tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
					has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
				}
				white_peace = FRA
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					728 = {
						owner = {
							tag = FRA
						}
						controller = {
							has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
							has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 728
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					670 = {
						owner = {
							tag = FRA
						}
						controller = {
							has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
							has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 670
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					671 = {
						owner = {
							tag = FRA
						}
						controller = {
							has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
							has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 671
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					286 = {
						owner = {
							tag = FRA
						}
						controller = {
							has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
							has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 286
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					741 = {
						owner = {
							tag = FRA
						}
						controller = {
							has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
							has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 741
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.64.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.74.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_global_flag = CHI_warred_with_JAP
				NOT = {
					FROM = {
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
					country_exists = PRC
				}
				FROM = {
					has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord_after_civil_war
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@CHI > 0 }
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@CHI > 19 }
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@CHI > 39 }
				add = 4
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@CHI > 59 }
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@CHI > 79 }
				add = 6
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = MEN
				JAP = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = PRC
				PRC = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = {
					has_country_flag = refused_shx_offer
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GXC
				has_global_flag = liangguang_solved
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@CHI > 89 }
				add = 1000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					tag = SHX
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				SHX = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Yen Hsi-shan"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = FROM
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = shx_sumitted
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					tag = GXC
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GXC = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Li Tsung-jen"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = FROM
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = gxc_sumitted
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					tag = YUN
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				YUN = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Lung Yun"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = FROM
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = yun_sumitted
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					tag = XSM
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				XSM = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Ma Pu-fang"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = FROM
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = xsm_sumitted
			}
		}
		
		
		
		
		
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.75 }
			annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.74.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				tag = MEN
				JAP = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
		}

				}
			}

			}

						create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}

		}

#ask sov to integrate sik
country_event = {
	id = kmt.84
	title = kmt.84.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
			}
		}
		text = kmt.84.d_1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
		}
		text = kmt.84.d_2
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_japanese_pact

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #declare war
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		name = kmt.84.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			else = {
				add_political_power = 50
			}
		}
				create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
			target = SIK
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = { #send demand first
		name = kmt.84.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = KMT_sik_refused_demand
			}
		}
		SIK = { country_event = { id = kmt.483 } }
	}

	option = { #send request faction leader help
		name = kmt.84.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT
					tag = SIK
				}
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = SIK
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = SIK
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.485 }
		}
	}

	option = { #i dont care
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		name = kmt.84.e
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = -0.2
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				is_owned_by = SIK
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
			set_variable = { KMT_is_not_central_core@ROOT = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			base = 0
		}

		add_stability = 0.01
		add_political_power = 100
	}

#response of seek peace
country_event = {
	id = kmt.186
	title = kmt.186.t
	desc = kmt.186.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_nationalist_china_machinegun_firing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		name = kmt.186.a
		white_peace = FROM
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.187 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		name = kmt.186.b
		white_peace = CHI
		set_country_flag = peace_and_factioned
		set_country_flag = china.101_fired
		set_global_flag = KMT_united_front_enabled
		set_global_flag = CHI_unite
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PRC
			}
			set_country_flag = PRC_joined_CHI_against_JAP
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = mao_is_greatest
						}
					}
				}
				PRC = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = unstable_alliance } }
				FROM = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = PRC modifier = unstable_alliance } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = KMT_fusze_to_yenan } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = KMT_use_postal_romanisation
					}
					set_province_name = { id = 8049 name = KMT_VP_8049_yenan_postal }
					else = {
						set_province_name = { id = 8049 name = KMT_VP_8049_yenan_pinyin }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = SOV } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = china.104_PRC_SOV_reinforcements
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = PRC_found_our_nation
						}
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					set_cosmetic_tag = GCDsgn
					load_oob = "PRC_SOV_reinforcements"
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				create_faction = chinese_united_front
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = joined_kmt
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
			}
			FROM = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			ROOT = { white_peace = PREV }
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.187 }
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.570 hours = 2 }
			}
		}
		add_to_war = {
			targeted_alliance = FROM
			enemy = JAP
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		name = kmt.186.c
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.188 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		name = kmt.186.e
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.188 }
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.189 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

			if = { limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } } add_to_faction = ROOT }
			country_event = { id = kmt.198 }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = FROM
			}
			remove_core_of = FROM
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = FROM
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = chi_tib_diplomatic_focus }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_nolonger_inalienable
			remove_from_array = { FROM.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
			remove_claim_by = FROM
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = FROM
				}
				TIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		#update_cg_inalienable_parts = yes
		set_global_flag = CHI_TIB_friend
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.197.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				has_wargoal_against = FROM
				add = 100
			}
		}

		}

	trigger = {

					exists = yes

					}
				}
				tag = PRC

				CHI = {
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = PRC
					}
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_puppet_of = PRC
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				CHI = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = PRC
					}
				}
				tag = CHI
				has_idea = KMT_chinese_matter
				PRC = {
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = CHI
					}
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_puppet_of = CHI
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.202.a
		dismantle_faction = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = kmt_planning_the_civil_war
			}
			remove_ideas = kmt_planning_the_civil_war
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_chinese_matter
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_chinese_matter
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.216
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				NOT = {
					state = 524
				}
				check_variable = { KMT_retreat_to_TW@ROOT = 1 }
				CONTROLLER = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						AND = {
							ROOT = { tag = CHI }
							has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		owns_state = 524
		has_full_control_of_state = 524
		NOT = { has_global_flag = status_quo_fired }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CHI
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_state = {
							check_variable = { KMT_retreat_to_TW@ROOT = 1 }
							CONTROLLER = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = ROOT
									is_subject_of = ROOT
									tag = ROOT
									has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
								}
								has_war_with = PRC
							}
						}
					}
					owns_state = 524
					has_full_control_of_state = 524
				}
				PRC = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.217 days = 15 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_state = {
								check_variable = { KMT_retreat_to_TW@ROOT = 1 }
								CONTROLLER = {
									OR = {
										is_in_faction_with = ROOT
										is_subject_of = ROOT
										tag = ROOT
									}
									has_war_with = CHI
								}
							}
						}
						owns_state = 524
						has_full_control_of_state = 524
					}
					CHI = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.217 days = 15 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

#status quo force peace
country_event = {
	id = kmt.217
	title = kmt.217.t
	desc = kmt.217.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_idea = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
			owns_state = 524
			has_full_control_of_state = 524
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				check_variable = { KMT_retreat_to_TW@FROM = 1 }
				CONTROLLER = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
						tag = FROM
						AND = {
							FROM = { tag = CHI }
							has_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
						}
					}
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = status_quo_fired
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 95
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				factor = 1.25
			}
		}
		name = kmt.217.a
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				remove_ideas = PRC_land_reform_stimulated_our_farmers
				remove_ideas = KMT_harsh_takeover
				remove_ideas = KMT_purge_collaborators
				remove_ideas = KMT_chinese_matter
				remove_ideas = KMT_collaborate_with_collaborators
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
					}
					remove_ideas = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						tag = CHI
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = TWKMT
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = FROM
							is_in_faction_with = FROM
							tag = FROM
						}
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					check_variable = { KMT_retreat_to_TW@FROM = 1 }
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					KOR = { is_puppet_of = FROM }
				}
				puppet = KOR
				KOR = {
					country_event = { id = wd.1 }
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_puppet_of = FROM
				}
				country_event = { id = wd.1 }
			}
			remove_ideas = kmt_planning_the_civil_war
		}
		white_peace = FROM
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = FROM
					is_subject_of = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		FROM = { set_country_flag = KMT_retreated_to_taiwan }
		set_global_flag = forced_ggnz_peace
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.386 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KMT_retreat_to_TW@FROM = 1 }
				}
				add_core_of = FROM
				remove_claim_by = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.217.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				factor = 0.1
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = PRC_take_taiwan
			days = 400
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			bonus = 0.33
			uses = 4
			category = naval_equipment
			category = air_equipment
			category = marine_tech
			category = para_tech
		}
	}
}

		text = kmt.221.d_2
		trigger = {
			has_government = neutrality
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_journalists_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.221.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					set_country_flag = JAP_new_faction_placeholder
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			create_faction = daitoa_kyoeiken
			add_to_faction = FROM
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = JAP_new_faction_placeholder
						is_puppet_of = JAP
						is_puppet_of = FROM
					}
				}
				add_to_faction = PREV
				clr_country_flag = JAP_new_faction_placeholder
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				id = FROM
				type = alliance
				value = 250
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				id = FROM
				type = befriend
				value = 250
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.478 }
			}
			news_event = { id = kns.6 hours = 3 }
			#PRC = {
			#	country_event = { id = chi_jap.1 hours = 5 }
			#}
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {
						has_idea = JAP_kodoha_idea
					}
				}
				JAP = {
					remove_country_leader_trait = JAP_kodoha_trait
					add_country_leader_trait = JAP_kodoha_trait_chi_ally
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {
						has_idea = JAP_toseiha_idea
					}
				}
				JAP = {
					remove_country_leader_trait = JAP_toseiha_trait
					add_country_leader_trait = JAP_toseiha_trait_chi_ally
				}
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 5 name = chi_jap_alliance_threat }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = KMT_jap_accepts_chi_into_faction
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_in_array = { FROM.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
						NOT = {
							tag = FROM
						}
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						PREV = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = PREV
								OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				remove_from_array = { FROM.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
				remove_core_of = FROM
				remove_claim_by = FROM
				#update_cg_inalienable_parts = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.221.c
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.222 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				has_idea = JAP_kodoha_idea
				factor = 0
			}
		}

			value = -250
		}

		}

					}

		has_global_flag = XSM_revived

		XSM = { exists = yes }
		NOT = { tag = XSM }
		tag = CHI
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.271.a
		annex_country = {
			target = XSM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			XSM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Ma Pu-fang"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					retire_country_leader = yes
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#wartime corruption
country_event = {
	id = kmt.272
	title = kmt.272.t
	desc = kmt.272.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers

	trigger = {
		any_country = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					#tag = HYQ
				}
			}
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
			has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.272.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
				add_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
				add_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
			}
		}
	}
}

#wartime corruption end
country_event = {
	id = kmt.273
	title = kmt.273.t
	desc = kmt.273.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
			has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
		}
		has_war = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.272.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
				add_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
					add_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#neutrality election
country_event = {
	id = kmt.279
	title = kmt.279.t
	desc = kmt.279.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
		}
	}

	#choose Chiang
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_global_flag = KMT_chiang_dead
			}
		}
		name = kmt.279.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = KMT_implement_parliamentary_system
				}
				any_state = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 150
			else = {
				add_political_power = 300
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.279.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				factor = 120
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Li Tsung-jen"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					army_experience = 50
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yu-hsiang"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										has_government = democratic
									}
									democratic > 0.6
								}
								set_politics = {
									ruling_party = democratic
									elections_allowed = yes
								}
								set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = democratic
								popularity = 0.1
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_government = democratic
								}
								create_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yu-hsiang"
									picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
									desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
									expire = "2060.1.1"
									ideology = conservatism
									traits = {
										#
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								add_political_power = -50
								add_popularity = {
									ideology = democratic
									popularity = -0.05
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.279.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				democratic > 0.6
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				factor = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ch'u Cheng"
				desc = "POLITICS_JU_ZHENG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Ju_Zheng.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					KMT_dislike_communism
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ch'u Cheng"
				desc = "POLITICS_JU_ZHENG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Ju_Zheng.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
					KMT_dislike_communism
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen

country_event = {
	id = kmt.282
	title = kmt.282.t
	desc = kmt.282.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		NOT = { has_idea = KMT_fight_for_survival }
		has_defensive_war = yes
		OR = {
			surrender_progress > 0.29
			AND = {
				608 = {
					controller = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
				613 = {
					controller = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = KMT_realisation
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = KMT_fight_for_survival
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.282.a

		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = KMT_fight_for_survival
		}
	}
}

#reform the army
country_event = {
	id = kmt.285
	title = kmt.285.t
	desc = kmt.285.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = CHI
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_weak_army
			has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
			has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
		}
		has_army_experience > 349
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = KMT_weak_army
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = KMT_weak_army
					add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
							add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
								}
								remove_ideas = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			army_experience = -500
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.285.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
					add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = KMT_weak_army
							add_idea = KMT_weak_army_lesser
						}
						else = {
							remove_ideas = KMT_weak_army_lesserer
						}
					}
				}
			}
			army_experience = -500
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		name = kmt.292.a

						}
					}
				}

					target = ROOT
					modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_detained
				}
				else = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = ROOT
						modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_detained_SOV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				same_ideo_with_USA = yes
				factor = 75
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = USA
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		name = kmt.292.b
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.294 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_help
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.296 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_help_JAP_reaction
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				factor = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		name = kmt.292.c
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.297 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_given_to_JAP
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.298 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_help_arrest
			}
		}
	}

#Annex warlords when they capitulate
country_event = {
	id = kmt.300
	title = kmt.300.t
	desc = kmt.300.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_political_power = 75
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = FROM
				}
				cancel_resistance = FROM
				start_resistance = ROOT
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = FROM
						is_core_of = FROM
					}
				}
				remove_claim_by = FROM
				remove_core_of = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.300.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 75
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#join KMT against PRC
country_event = {
	id = kmt.301
	title = kmt.301.t
	desc = {
		text = kmt.301.d_1
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.301.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	trigger = {
		always = no
		PRC = {
			num_of_controlled_states > 5
			has_war_with = CHI
		}
		OR = {
			tag = SHX
			tag = YUN
		
			tag = GXC
			tag = XSM
			
			
			
			tag = QIA
			
			
			tag = CHI
		}
		NOT = {
			tag = CHI
		}
		CHI = {
			has_war_with = PRC
			is_puppet = no
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_pro_japanese_coup
				has_country_flag = KMT_red_coup_finish
			}
		}
		PRC = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_PRC_joined
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = KMT_PRC_joined
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.301.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = CHI
				enemy = PRC
			}
			set_country_flag = joined_kmt_against_prc
			CHI = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.302 }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				PRC = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.302 }
					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.301.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#scorch earth
country_event = {
	id = kmt.328
	title = kmt.328.t
	desc = kmt.328.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	trigger = {
		always = no
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_1
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_2
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_3
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_4
		}
		any_state = {
			is_owned_by = ROOT
			controller = {
				has_offensive_war_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				has_state_flag = scorched
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = scorched
					}
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = {
							arms_factory > 0
						}
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					set_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								PREV = {
									industrial_complex > 0
								}
							}
							remove_building = {
								type = industrial_complex
								level = 1
							}
							set_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
						}
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = scorched
				set_state_flag = scorched_tt
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.328.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorched_tt
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorched_tt
				}
				clr_state_flag = scorched_tt
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
				}
				clr_state_flag = scorch_removed_ic_tt
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
				}
				clr_state_flag = scorch_removed_af_tt
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		if = {

				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			FROM = {
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}

		if = {

		}
	}

			base = 50
		}

			has_global_flag = KMT_seek_cob
		}
		if = {

					is_ai = no
				}
			}

					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}

						set_nationality = CHI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.346 hours = 2 }
		}
	}
}

#retreat to taiwan
country_event = {
	id = kmt.347
	title = kmt.347.t
	desc = kmt.347.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		always = no
		has_full_control_of_state = 524
		tag = CHI
		PRC = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			is_puppet = no
		}
		OR = {
			num_of_controlled_states < 4
			surrender_progress > 0.79
		}
		has_global_flag = PRC_restart_chinese_civil_war
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 80
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		name = kmt.347.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
				NOT = {
					state = 524
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		add_ideas = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
		set_capital = {
			state = 524
		}
		add_political_power = -50
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		name = kmt.347.b
	}
}

#meeting with KOR RYU
country_event = {
	id = kmt.356
	title = kmt.356.t
	desc = kmt.356.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = CHI
		is_puppet = no
		OR = {
			KOR = {
				exists = yes
				is_puppet = no
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = refused_CHI_friendship
						has_country_flag = accepted_CHI_friendship
					}
				}
			}
			RYU = {
				exists = yes
				is_puppet = no
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = refused_CHI_friendship
						has_country_flag = accepted_CHI_friendship
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = pending_CHI_meet
			has_global_flag = meeting_fired
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 20 }

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = pending_CHI_meet
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.356.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					exists = yes
					is_puppet = no
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = refused_CHI_friendship
							has_country_flag = accepted_CHI_friendship
						}
					}
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.357 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RYU = {
					exists = yes
					is_puppet = no
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = refused_CHI_friendship
							has_country_flag = accepted_CHI_friendship
						}
					}
				}
			}
			RYU = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.357 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = kmt.356.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = kmt_meet_first_fire
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 100
			set_country_flag = kmt_meet_first_fire
		}
		set_global_flag = meeting_fired
		clr_global_flag = pending_CHI_meet
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.357
	title = kmt.357.t
	desc = kmt.357.d

				target = ROOT
				modifier = CHI_KR_fd
			}

				limit = {
					tag = KOR
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "KOR"
					value = 50
				}

					type = alliance
					id = "KOR"
					value = 50

country_event = {

	title = kmt.367.t
	desc = kmt.367.d

		always = no

			has_war_with = JAP
		}

			OR = {
				region = 155
				state = 610

			}

	desc = kmt.368.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		}
		name = kmt.368.a

			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_harsh_takeover_prc_purge
				days = 700
			}
			else = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = KMT_harsh_takeover_prc
					days = 600
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_stability = -0.05
	}

	option = {

			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Li Tsung-jen"
				desc = "POLITICS_LI_ZONGREN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/GXC/Portrait_Guanxi_Clique_Li_Zongren.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"

				traits = {
					KMT_lzr_defensive_focus
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Li Tsung-jen"
				desc = "POLITICS_LI_ZONGREN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/GXC/Portrait_Guanxi_Clique_Li_Zongren.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = fascism_ideology
				traits = {
					KMT_lzr_defensive_focus
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			annex_country = {
				target = GXC
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Li Tsung-jen"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					retire_country_leader = yes
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.371 }
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = cks_retire
	}

	option = {

			base = 5
		}
		name = kmt.370.b

			idea = KMT_chiang_li_rivalry
			days = 300

		}
	}

				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = CHI
		has_war_with = JAP
		671 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		670 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		741 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
		286 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			is_owned_by = JAP
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	#liberate all
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		name = kmt.389.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LAO
			}
			LAO = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = VIN
			}
			VIN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAM
			}
			CAM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = LAO
					tag = VIN
					tag = CAM
				}
			}
			give_military_access = ROOT
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_indochina_liberator
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_damaged_colonial_interest
			}
		}
	}

	#puppet all
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		name = kmt.389.b
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LAO
			}
			LAO = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = VIN
			}
			VIN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAM
			}
			CAM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = LAO
					tag = VIN
					tag = CAM
				}
			}
			give_military_access = ROOT
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_indochina_liberator
			}
			ROOT = {
				puppet = PREV
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_damaged_colonial_interest
			}
		}
	}

	#back to france
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		name = kmt.389.c
		FRA = {
			transfer_state = 671
			transfer_state = 670
			transfer_state = 741
			transfer_state = 286
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_returned_indochina
			}
			give_military_access = ROOT
		}
	}

	#nothing
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 8 }
		name = kmt.389.e
	}
}

#chi civil war
country_event = {
	id = kmt.392
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = KMT_special_japan16_civil_war
			has_civil_war = yes
		}
		any_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_government = neutrality
						ROOT = { has_government = neutrality }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = democratic
						ROOT = { has_government = democratic }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = communism
						ROOT = { has_government = communism }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = fascism
						ROOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = kmt392_fired
				has_global_flag = xian_civil_war
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = kmt392_fired
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = PRC
					has_idea = cg_warlords
				}
				is_puppet = no
				has_civil_war = no
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.393 }
		}
	}

	option = {
	}
}

#chi civil war
country_event = {
	id = kmt.393
	title = kmt.393.t
	desc = kmt.393.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = PRC
			has_idea = cg_warlords
		}
		is_puppet = no
		has_civil_war = no
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = CHI
					has_civil_war = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				any_country = {
					original_tag = CHI
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_war_together_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 49
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				has_government = fascism
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				has_government = neutrality
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				has_government = communism
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				has_government = democratic
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Wang Ching-wei"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add = -500
			}
		}
		name = kmt.393.a
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_war_with = FROM
				NOT = {
					tag = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = FROM
					enemy = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 49
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					original_tag = CHI
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = fascism
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					original_tag = CHI
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = fascism
				}
				has_government = fascism
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					original_tag = CHI
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				has_government = neutrality
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					original_tag = CHI
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = communism
				}
				has_government = communism
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					original_tag = CHI
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_government = democratic
				}
				has_government = democratic
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					original_tag = CHI
					has_war_with = FROM
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Wang Ching-wei"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add = -500
			}
		}
		name = kmt.393.b
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_war_with = FROM
				NOT = {
					tag = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = PREV
					enemy = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.393.c
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				has_civil_war = yes
				has_war_with = FROM
				NOT = {
					tag = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.393.e
	}
}

#neutrality election
country_event = {
	id = kmt.397
	title = kmt.279.t
	desc = kmt.397.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
		}
	}

	#choose Chiang
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_global_flag = KMT_chiang_dead
			}
		}
		name = kmt.279.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.279.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				factor = 120
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Li Tsung-jen"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					army_experience = 50
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.05
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yu-hsiang"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										has_government = democratic
									}
									democratic > 0.6
								}
								set_politics = {
									ruling_party = democratic
									elections_allowed = yes
								}
								set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = democratic
								popularity = 0.1
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_government = democratic
								}
								create_country_leader = {
									name = "Feng Yu-hsiang"
									picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
									desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
									expire = "2060.1.1"
									ideology = conservatism
									traits = {
										#
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										has_country_leader = {
											name = "Ch'u Cheng"
											ruling_only = yes
										}
									}
									add_popularity = {
										ideology = democratic
										popularity = -0.03
									}
									add_popularity = {
										ideology = communism
										popularity = -0.05
									}
									else = {
										add_political_power = -50
										add_popularity = {
											ideology = democratic
											popularity = -0.05
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.397.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				democratic > 0.6
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				factor = 50
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Xu Fulin"
				desc = "POLITICS_XU_FULIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Xu Fulin"
				desc = "POLITICS_XU_FULIN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#chiang died
country_event = {
	id = kmt.399
	title = kmt.399.t
	desc = {
		text = kmt.399.d
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Yen Chia-kan"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.399.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Yen Chia-kan"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral

	trigger = {
		date > 1975.4.1
		tag = CHI
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = KMT_chiang_dead
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader = 1001
				}
				remove_unit_leader = 1001
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader = 10011
				}
				remove_unit_leader = 10011
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = KMT_chiang_die_as_president
				kill_country_leader = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Yen Chia-kan"
						desc = "POLITICS_YEN_CHIA-KAN_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = oligarchism
						traits = {
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Yen Chia-kan"
						desc = "POLITICS_YEN_CHIA-KAN_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = conservatism
						traits = {
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.399.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_chiang_die_as_president
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Yen Chia-kan"
						desc = "POLITICS_YEN_CHIA-KAN_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = oligarchism
						traits = {
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Yen Chia-kan"
						desc = "POLITICS_YEN_CHIA-KAN_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_2.dds"
						expire = "2060.1.1"
						ideology = conservatism
						traits = {
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

#elections
country_event = {
	id = kmt.401
	title = kmt.279.t
	desc = kmt.397.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Yen Chia-kan"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			has_government = democratic
		}
		has_country_flag = KMT_second_election_passed
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = cks_killed_xian
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_global_flag = KMT_chiang_dead
			}
		}
		name = kmt.279.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					KMT_cks_generallissimo
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.279.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Li Tsung-jen"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			army_experience = 50
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Feng Yu-hsiang"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = democratic
							}
							democratic > 0.6
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = democratic
							elections_allowed = yes
						}
						set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Feng Yu-hsiang"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
							desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
							expire = "2060.1.1"
							ideology = conservatism
							traits = {
								#
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Ch'u Cheng"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = democratic
								popularity = -0.03
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = communism
								popularity = -0.05
							}
							else = {
								add_political_power = -50
								add_popularity = {
									ideology = democratic
									popularity = -0.05
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.401.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				democratic > 0.6
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
	}
}

#bandits
country_event = {
	id = kmt.415
	title = kmt.415.t
	desc = kmt.415.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	trigger = {
		has_idea = KMT_PRC_bandits
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
				days > 30
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 25 }

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
		set_country_flag = KMT_PRC_bandits_cooldown
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.414.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					any_neighbor_state = {
						controller = {
							has_idea = KMT_PRC_bandits
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						controller = {
							has_idea = KMT_PRC_bandits
						}
					}
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 0
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						damage = 1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					damage_building = {
						type = infrastructure
						damage = 4
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							industrial_complex > 0
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							damage = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		has_global_flag = KMT_PRC_deserters_disarm
	}
