	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.416.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
		hidden_effect = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Min Bing"
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"You Ji Dui\" division_template = \"Min Bing\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 0.35"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"You Ji Dui\" division_template = \"Min Bing\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 0.35"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"You Ji Dui\" division_template = \"Min Bing\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 0.35"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"You Ji Dui\" division_template = \"Min Bing\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 0.35"
					owner = ROOT
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"You Ji Dui\" division_template = \"Min Bing\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 0.35"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_ex_commie_peasant_forces_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.416.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		add_ideas = KMT_ex_commie_partisans
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.416.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}


#Sichuan famine in 1936
country_event = {
	id = kmt.417
	title = kmt.299.t
	desc = kmt.417.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	trigger = {
		controls_state = 605
		date > 1936.2.25
		date < 1938.1.1
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.417.a
		trigger = {
			has_idea = cg_warlords
			any_country = {
				tag = CHI
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = CHI
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.299 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				tag = CHI
				factor = 95
			}
		}
		name = kmt.299.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_sichuan_famine_no_aid
			days = 350
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		name = kmt.299.b
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_sichuan_famine_aid
			days = 350
		}
	}
}

#change mck city names
country_event = {
	id = kmt.421
	title = kmt.421.t
	desc = kmt.421.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_001

	trigger = {
		always = no
		OR = {
			tag = CHI
			AND = {
				tag = PRC
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = PRC_found_our_nation
					has_completed_focus = PRC_the_second_northeast_flag_replacement
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				owns_state = 750
				750 = {
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = renaming_decided
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 328
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided1567
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 716
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided11771
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 524
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided12068
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.421.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				750 = {
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = renaming_decided
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = KMT_use_postal_romanisation
				}
				750 = { set_state_name = KMT_1150_postal }
				else = {
					750 = { set_state_name = VICTORY_POINTS_1150 }
				}
			}
			750 = {
				set_state_flag = renaming_decided
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided12068
				}
				524 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = KMT_use_postal_romanisation
				}
				set_province_name = { id = 12068 name = KMT_12068_postal }
				else = {
					set_province_name = { id = 12068 name = VICTORY_POINTS_12068 }
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = renaming_decided12068
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided1567
				}
				328 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_province_name = { id = 1567 name = KMT_changchun }
			set_global_flag = renaming_decided1567
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided11771
				}
				716 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_province_name = { id = 11771 name = KMT_shenyang }
			set_global_flag = renaming_decided11771
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.421.b
		add_political_power = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				750 = {
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = renaming_decided
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			750 = {
				set_state_flag = renaming_decided
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided1567
				}
				328 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = renaming_decided1567
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided11771
				}
				716 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = renaming_decided11771
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = renaming_decided12068
				}
				524 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = renaming_decided12068
		}
	}
}

	id = kmt.422
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		is_chinese_nations = yes
		owns_state = 728
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

				has_global_flag = KMT_use_postal_romanisation
			}
			728 = { set_state_name = "Xinhui" } 
			else = {
				728 = { set_state_name = "Maoming" }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.423
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
				value = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			modify_global_flag = {
				flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.424
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = KMT_check_non_ai_chinese_player_flag
					value < 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_chinese_nations = yes
						NOT = { tag = SIK }
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_chinese_nations = yes
						NOT = { tag = SIK }
						is_ai = no
					}
					country_event = { id = kmt.420 }
				}
				else = {
					CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.420 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.424.a
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.430
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			# WJW = {
			# 	is_puppet_of = JAP
			# 	exists = yes
			# }
			CHI = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			any_country = {
				is_chinese_nations = yes
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				exists = yes
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				# WJW = {
				# 	exists = yes
				# 	OR = {
				# 		is_puppet_of = JAP
				# 		is_in_faction_with = JAP
				# 	}
				# }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_chinese_nations = yes
						#tag = HYQ
					}
					exists = yes
					NOT = { tag = SIK }
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					#NOT = { tag = WJW }
				}
				# WJW = {
				# 	annex_country = {
				# 		target = PREV
				# 		transfer_troops = no
				# 	}
				# }
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						# HYQ = {
						# 	exists = yes
						# 	OR = {
						# 		is_puppet_of = JAP
						# 		is_in_faction_with = JAP
						# 	}
						# }
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_chinese_nations = yes
								#tag = WJW
							}
							exists = yes
							NOT = { tag = SIK }
							is_puppet_of = JAP
							#NOT = { tag = HYQ }
						}
						# HYQ = {
						# 	annex_country = {
						# 		target = PREV
						# 		transfer_troops = no
						# 	}
						# }
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								CHI = {
									exists = yes
									OR = {
										is_puppet_of = JAP
										is_in_faction_with = JAP
									}
								}
							}
							every_country = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										is_chinese_nations = yes
										# tag = WJW
										# tag = HYQ
									}
									exists = yes
									NOT = { tag = SIK }
									is_puppet_of = JAP
									NOT = { tag = CHI }
								}
								CHI = {
									annex_country = {
										target = PREV
										transfer_troops = no
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								random_country = {
									limit = {
										is_chinese_nations = yes
										is_subject_of = JAP
									}
									save_event_target_as = KMT_JAP_temp_annex_actor
								}
								every_country = {
									limit = {
										is_chinese_nations = yes
										exists = yes
										NOT = { tag = SIK }
										is_puppet_of = JAP
										NOT = { tag = event_target:KMT_JAP_temp_annex_actor }
										NOT = { tag = CHI }
									}
									event_target:KMT_JAP_temp_annex_actor = {
										annex_country = {
											target = PREV
											transfer_troops = no
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {}
}


#aaa
country_event = {
	id = kmt.431
	hidden = yes


	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
				NOT = { tag = CHI }
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
			ROOT = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 5
			fascism = 5
			communism = 1
			neutrality = 89
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = KMT_pro_jap_action_count
					value > 0
				}
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = KMT_pro_jap_action_count
					value < 3
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Feng Yu-hsiang"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Feng_Yuxiang.dds"
				desc = "POLITICS_FENG_YUXIANG_DESC"
				expire = "2060.1.1"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
					#
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_China_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC_DESC"
					expire = "2060.1.1"
					ideology = despotism
					traits = {
						KMT_cks_generallissimo
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {}
}

			}

		}
	}

		name = kmt.434.a
	}

#warlord faction
country_event = {
	id = kmt.435
	title = kmt.435.t
	desc = kmt.435.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured

	trigger = {
		always = no
		CHI = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord_after_civil_war
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord
			}
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = cg_warlords
			has_idea = cg_warlords
			has_idea = cg_warlords
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event
			has_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader
			has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					has_idea = cg_warlords
					has_idea = cg_warlords
				}
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
				}
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			CHI = {
				OR = {
					has_wargoal_against = PREV
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}

			OR = {
				has_idea = cg_warlords
				has_idea = cg_warlords
				has_idea = cg_warlords
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.434.a
		create_faction = "anti_alliance"
		set_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
		clr_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.434.a
		set_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader
		clr_global_flag = pending_warlord_faction_event
	}
}

#warlord faction
country_event = {
	id = kmt.436
	title = kmt.435.t
	desc = kmt.435.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured

	trigger = {
		always = no
		CHI = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord_after_civil_war
				has_completed_focus = KMT_warlord
			}
			has_war_with = ROOT
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = cg_warlords
			has_idea = cg_warlords
			has_idea = cg_warlords
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader
		}
		any_country = {
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			CHI = {
				OR = {
					has_wargoal_against = PREV
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
			}
			OR = {
				has_idea = cg_warlords
				has_idea = cg_warlords
				has_idea = cg_warlords
			}
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.434.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
				}
				create_faction = "anti_alliance"
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = warlord_faction_leader
			}
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.434.a
		set_country_flag = dont_want_be_warlord_faction_leader
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.442
	title = kmt.442.t
	desc = kmt.442.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_officers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.442.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = no
			}
			818 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		FROM = { country_event = { id = kmt.443 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.442.a

#force red coup
country_event = {
	id = kmt.479
	title = kmt.479.t
	desc = kmt.479.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_nationalist_china_machinegun_firing

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = KMT_privilege_to_proletarians
			focus_progress = {
				focus = KMT_privilege_to_proletarians
				progress > 0
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = KMT_invite_chen_duxiu
			NOT = {
				focus_progress = {
					focus = KMT_invite_chen_duxiu
					progress > 0
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = KMT_help_mao_infiltrate
			NOT = {
				focus_progress = {
					focus = KMT_help_mao_infiltrate
					progress > 0
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = {
			flag = KMT_finished_a_communist_focus
			days > 350
		}
		OR = {
			has_war = no
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = KMT_finished_another_communist_focus }
			has_global_flag = {
				flag = KMT_finished_another_communist_focus
				days > 30
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			AND = {
				has_offensive_war_with = PRC
				has_global_flag = KMT_PRC_agrees_to_work_with_us
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			AND = {
				has_defensive_war_with = PRC
				has_global_flag = KMT_PRC_agrees_to_work_with_us
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			KMT_red_coup_effect_procrastinated = yes
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.479.a
	}
}

		}
	}

					has_idea = KMT_into_mao_2
				}
				remove_ideas = KMT_into_mao_2

	id = kmt.499

	desc = kmt.499.d

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_war = no
		has_global_flag = KMT_finished_a_communist_focus

			has_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao_idea
			has_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao2_idea
			has_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao3_idea
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao_idea
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_into_mao
				clr_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao_idea
				set_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao2_idea
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_into_mao_2
				clr_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao2_idea
				set_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao3_idea
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_into_mao_3
				clr_country_flag = KMT_has_into_mao3_idea
				set_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.499.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_into_mao
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao2
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_into_mao_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao3
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_into_mao_3
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao
		clr_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao2
		clr_country_flag = KMT_return_into_mao3
	}
}

#ledo road
country_event = {
	id = kmt.514
	title = kmt.507.t
	desc = kmt.514.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_british_artillery

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = USA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CHI
		}
		exists = yes
		has_capitulated = no
		is_puppet = no
		is_alone_or_in_faction_at_peace_with_CHI = yes
		has_idea = KMT_assistance_to_CHI
		CHI = {
			exists = yes
			is_puppet = no
			has_defensive_war_with = JAP
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						is_controlled_by = PREV
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.24
				AND = {
					613 = {
						controller = { has_war_with = CHI }
					}
					608 = {
						controller = { has_war_with = CHI }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			is_puppet_of = JAP
			is_in_faction_with = JAP
			has_non_aggression_pact_with = JAP
			has_war_with = CHI
			is_puppet_of = CHI
		}
		640 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
			}
		}
		791 = {
			controller = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_war_with = USA
				}
			}
		}
		747 = {
			controller = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_war_with = USA
				}
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
					is_puppet_of = CHI
					has_war_together_with = CHI
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.514.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_opinion = {
						target = CHI
						value < -69
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				791 = {
					controller = {
						is_puppet = yes
					}
				}
			}
			791 = {
				controller = {
					overlord = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.515 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				791 = {
					controller = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.515 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_war_with = CHI
					has_opinion = {
						target = CHI
						value < -69
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		name = kmt.507.b
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.527
	title = kmt.527.t
	desc = kmt.527.d

		has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		VIN = {
			has_war_with = CHI
			has_capitulated = yes
			is_puppet = yes

				capital_scope = {
					NOT = {

					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

		SIA = {
			has_war_with = CHI
			has_capitulated = yes
			is_puppet = yes
			overlord = {
				capital_scope = {
					NOT = {
						is_on_continent = asia
					}
				}
			}
		}
		tag = CHI

country_event = {

		has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = RAJ
			owner = {
				NOT = { tag = RAJ }
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		RAJ = {
			exists = no
		}
		tag = CHI
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = {

				limit = {

					}
					is_core_of = RAJ
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = RAJ
					}
				}

					transfer_state = PREV
				}

#took raj land
country_event = {
	id = kmt.535
	title = kmt.535.t
	desc = kmt.535.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		country_exists = RAJ
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = RAJ
			owner = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				NOT = { tag = RAJ }
			}
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		tag = CHI
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			RAJ = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						controller = {
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
								is_puppet_of = ROOT
							}
						}
						is_core_of = RAJ
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = RAJ
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = liberated_raj_state
					RAJ = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_first_time_land_return_thru_otc }
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Milishiya"
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = KMT_first_time_land_return_thru_otc
				}
				event_target:liberated_raj_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Milishiya\" division_template = \"Milishiya\" start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = RAJ
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Milishiya\" division_template = \"Milishiya\" start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = RAJ
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Milishiya\" division_template = \"Milishiya\" start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = RAJ
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.535.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			RAJ = {
				transfer_state = event_target:liberated_raj_state
			}
		}
	}
}

#from withdraw support
country_event = {
	id = kmt.538
	title = kmt.538.t
	desc = kmt.538.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = ENG }
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_burma_road_idea
					has_idea = KMT_burma_road_idea_closed
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_burma_road_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_burma_road_idea_closed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = FRA }
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea
					has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea_closed
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea_closed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = USA }
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_ledo_road_idea
					has_idea = KMT_ledo_road_idea_closed
					has_idea = KMT_the_hump_idea
					has_idea = KMT_the_hump_idea_closed
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_ledo_road_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_ledo_road_idea_closed
			remove_ideas = KMT_the_hump_idea
			remove_ideas = KMT_the_hump_idea_closed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = GER }
				OR = {
					has_idea = german_advisors
					has_idea = KMT_sino_german_joint_research
					has_idea = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = german_advisors
			remove_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research
			remove_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = sino_german_cooperation
				target = GER
			}
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = more_sino_german_coop_trade
				target = GER
			}
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = more_sino_german_coop
				target = GER
			}
			GER = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = sino_german_cooperation
					target = CHI
				}
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = more_sino_german_coop_trade
					target = CHI
				}
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = more_sino_german_coop
					target = CHI
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_unit_leader = 1040 }
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 1040 }
					set_nationality = GER
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.538.a
	}
}


#communist revolution!
country_event = {
	id = kmt.539
	title = kmt.539.t
	desc = kmt.539.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.539.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				is_subject_of = FROM
				FROM = { has_government = communism }
				factor = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = fascism
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = yes
				NOT = { is_subject_of = FROM }
			}
			overlord = {
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
				end_puppet = ROOT
				country_event = { id = kmt.544 }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.5
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = KMT_communists_overthrow_white_peace_window_flag
			activate_mission = KMT_communists_overthrow_white_peace_window_mission
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.539.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					is_capital = no
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = FROM
				}
				FROM = {
					end_puppet = ROOT
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							has_government = communism
						}
						FROM = {
							puppet = PREV
						}
						declare_war_on = {
							target = ROOT
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
							create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
						target = ROOT
						type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					}
					country_event = { id = kmt.543 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#relate back to .430
country_event = {
	id = kmt.567
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			# WJW = {
			# 	is_puppet_of = JAP
			# 	exists = yes
			# }
			CHI = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			# HYQ = {
			# 	OR = {
			# 		is_puppet_of = JAP
			# 		is_in_faction_with = JAP
			# 	}
			# 	exists = yes
			# }
			any_country = {
				is_chinese_nations = yes
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_event_target = KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_chinese_nations = yes
							#tag = WJW
						}
						is_puppet_of = JAP
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							#tag = HYQ
						}
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				exists = yes
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = KMT_first_chinese_puppet_of_jap
		}
	}

	option = {}
}

#from demand peace
country_event = {
	id = kmt.577
	title = kmt.577.t
	desc = kmt.577.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { set_variable = { KMT_puppets_count = 0 } }

	#ok
	option = {
		name = kmt.577.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					surrender_progress > 0.5
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					surrender_progress > 0.75
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}

		#trigger agree event for demander if we own any of the demanded states
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					#if we own any demanded steppe states
					AND = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 2 } } #FROM has demanded steppe
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								region = 152 #central steppe
								region = 145 #central asia
							}
						}
					}
					#if we own any demanded indochina states
					AND = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 2 } } #FROM has demanded indochina
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 671 #tonkin
								state = 670 #laos
								state = 286 #cambodia
								state = 741 #southern indochina
							}
						}
					}
					#if we own any demanded trade ports
					AND = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 2 } } #FROM has demanded ports
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 729 #macau
								state = 728 #gzw
								state = 326 #hk
								state = 743 #tsingtao
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.578 } #agree event
			}
		}

		#mark states to be transfered
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 } #if we or any of our subjects own demanded states in indochina
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_from_owned_indochina_states_tt2
			hidden_effect = {
				#mark owned states to be transfered
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 671 #tonkin
							state = 670 #laos
							state = 286 #cambodia
							state = 741 #southern indochina
						}
					}
					set_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@ROOT = 1 } #set marked variable
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 } #if we or any of our subjects own demanded states in steppe
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_from_owned_steppe_states_tt2
			hidden_effect = {
				#mark owned states to be transfered
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 152 #central steppe
							region = 145 #central asia
						}
					}
					set_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@ROOT = 1 } #set marked variable
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 } #if we or any of our subjects own demanded ports
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_from_owned_ports_states_tt2
			hidden_effect = {
				#mark owned states to be transfered
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 729 #macau
							state = 728 #gzw
							state = 326 #hk
							state = 743 #tsingtao
						}
					}
					set_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@ROOT = 1 } #set marked variable
				}
			}
		}

		#if no subjects own demanded state, white peace immediately
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 0 } #FROM demanded indochina
						AND = {
							check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 } #we own demanded states in indochina
							NOT = { #our subjects do not own demanded states in indochina
								any_country = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
									any_owned_state = {
										OR = {
											state = 671
											state = 670
											state = 286
											state = 741
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 0 } #FROM demanded steppe
						AND = {
							check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 } #we own demanded states in steppe
							NOT = { #our subjects do not own demanded states in steppe
								any_country = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
									any_owned_state = {
										OR = {
											region = 152
											region = 145
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 0 } #FROM demanded ports
						AND = {
							check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 } #we own demanded ports
							NOT = { #our subjects do not own demanded ports
								any_country = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
									any_owned_state = {
										OR = {
											state = 729
											state = 728
											state = 743
											state = 326
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = FROM
		}

		#mark self as white peace target
		set_variable = { KMT_582_white_peace_target@ROOT = 1 }

		#prevent immature peace
		#only the last subject will trigger the peace and transfer state effect
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { ROOT.kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								region = 152
								region = 145
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { ROOT.kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 671
								state = 670
								state = 286
								state = 741
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { ROOT.kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 729
								state = 728
								state = 326
								state = 743
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.KMT_puppets_count = 1 }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { ROOT.kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								region = 152
								region = 145
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { ROOT.kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 671
								state = 670
								state = 286
								state = 741
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { ROOT.kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 729
								state = 728
								state = 326
								state = 743
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.580 }
		}
	}

	#no
	option = {
		name = kmt.577.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.579 }
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {

		}

				FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 } }
			}

			FROM = { set_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 0 } }
		}
	}

#give in or fight
#FROM.FROM = China
#FROM = overlord
country_event = {
	id = kmt.580
	title = kmt.580.t
	desc = kmt.580.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_panzer_attack

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 } }
			}
			set_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 } }
			}
			set_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 } }
			}
			set_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 }
		}
		FROM = { save_event_target_as = KMT_582_B }
		FROM.FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = KMT_582_A
		}
	}

	#give in
	option = {
		name = kmt.580.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:KMT_582_A
					ratio < 0.9
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:KMT_582_A
					ratio < 0.7
				}
				add = 10
			}
		}
		event_target:KMT_582_A = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.578 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_582_A = {
					check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 2 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_fromfrom_owned_indochina_states_tt2
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 671
						state = 670
						state = 286
						state = 741
					}
				}
				set_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@event_target:KMT_582_B = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_582_A = {
					check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 2 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_fromfrom_owned_steppe_states_tt2
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = 152
						region = 145
					}
				}
				set_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@event_target:kmt_582_b = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_582_A = {
					check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 2 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_transfer_all_fromfrom_owned_port_states_tt2
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 729
						state = 728
						state = 326
						state = 743
					}
				}
				set_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@event_target:kmt_582_b = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						event_target:KMT_582_A = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 0 } }
						AND = {
							event_target:KMT_582_A = {
								check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 2 }
							}
							NOT = {
								any_owned_state = {
									NOT = {
										state = 670
										state = 671
										state = 286
										state = 741
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						event_target:KMT_582_A = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 0 } }
						AND = {
							event_target:KMT_582_A = {
								check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 2 }
							}
							NOT = {
								any_owned_state = {
									NOT = {
										region = 145
										region = 152
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						event_target:KMT_582_A = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 0 } }
						AND = {
							event_target:KMT_582_A = {
								check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 2 }
							}
							NOT = {
								any_owned_state = {
									NOT = {
										state = 729
										state = 728
										state = 326
										state = 743
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
			else = {
				set_variable = { KMT_582_B.KMT_582_white_peace_target@ROOT = 1 }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				white_peace = event_target:KMT_582_A
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { KMT_582_B.KMT_puppets_count = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { KMT_582_B.KMT_puppets_count < 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@event_target:kmt_582_b = 1 }
					}
					event_target:KMT_582_A = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KMT_582_B.KMT_582_white_peace_target@THIS = 1 }
					}
					white_peace = event_target:KMT_582_A
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#
	option = {
		name = kmt.580.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:KMT_582_A
					ratio > 1.5
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:KMT_582_A
					ratio > 2
				}
				add = 10
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			end_puppet = ROOT
			country_event = { id = kmt.581 }
		}
		FROM.FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.579 }
		}
		# add_opinion_modifier = {
		# 	target = FROM
		# 	modifier = KMT_incompetent_gov_om
		# }
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				white_peace = FROM.FROM
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { KMT_582_B.KMT_puppets_count = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { KMT_582_B.KMT_puppets_count < 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KMT_582_to_be_transfered@event_target:kmt_582_b = 1 }
					}
					event_target:KMT_582_A = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KMT_582_B.KMT_582_white_peace_target@THIS = 1 }
					}
					white_peace = event_target:KMT_582_A
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#cut losses event
country_event = {
	id = kmt.583
	title = kmt.583.t
	desc = kmt.583.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { FROM.KMT_puppets_count2 = 0 }
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.583.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		set_variable = { FROM.KMT_584_white_peace_target@FROM = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 0 } }
						AND = {
							FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 } }
							NOT = {
								any_state = {
									OR = {
										state = 671
										state = 670
										state = 286
										state = 741
									}
									OWNER = {
										is_subject_of = FROM
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 0 } }
						AND = {
							FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 } }
							NOT = {
								any_state = {
									OR = {
										region = 145
										region = 152
									}
									OWNER = {
										is_subject_of = FROM
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 0 } }
						AND = {
							FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 } }
							NOT = {
								any_state = {
									OR = {
										state = 729
										state = 728
										state = 326
										state = 743
									}

										is_subject_of = FROM
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = FROM
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							region = 152
							region = 145
						}
						OWNER = {
							tag = FROM
							check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 671
							state = 670
							state = 286
							state = 741
						}
						OWNER = {
							tag = FROM
							check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 729
							state = 728
							state = 326
							state = 743
						}
						OWNER = {
							tag = FROM
							check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = FROM
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { FROM.kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								region = 152
								region = 145
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { FROM.kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 671
								state = 670
								state = 286
								state = 741
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { FROM.kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 729
								state = 728
								state = 326
								state = 743
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { FROM.KMT_puppets_count2 = 1 }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = FROM
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_indochina_war = 1 } }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 671
								state = 670
								state = 286
								state = 741
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_steppe_war = 1 } }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								region = 152
								region = 145
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 1 } }
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								state = 729
								state = 728
								state = 326
								state = 743
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = kmt.584
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.583.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.579 }
		}
	}
}

						AND = {
							event_target:KMT_582_A = {
								check_variable = { kmt_demand_ports_war = 2 }
							}
							NOT = {
								any_owned_state = {
									NOT = {
										state = 729
										state = 728
										state = 326
										state = 743
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
			else = {
				set_variable = { KMT_584_B.KMT_584_white_peace_target@ROOT = 1 }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				white_peace = event_target:KMT_584_A
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { KMT_584_B.KMT_puppets_count2 = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { KMT_584_B.KMT_puppets_count2 < 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KMT_584_to_be_transfered@event_target:kmt_584_b = 1 }
					}
					event_target:KMT_584_A = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KMT_584_B.KMT_584_white_peace_target@THIS = 1 }
					}
					white_peace = event_target:KMT_584_A
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#
	option = {
		name = kmt.580.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:KMT_584_A
					ratio > 1.5
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:KMT_584_A
					ratio > 2
				}
				add = 10
			}
		}
		FROM.FROM = {
			end_puppet = ROOT
			country_event = { id = kmt.581 }
		}
		FROM = {

						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }

				}
			}
			else = {

					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Waiji Zhiyuan Jun\" division_template = \"Foreign Volunteers\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1"

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = kmt.600.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.600.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 605
					state = 753
					state = 823
					state = 748
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
			add_core_of = FROM
			remove_core_of = ROOT
			remove_claim_by = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			set_capital = {
			state = 605
		}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			set_nationality = FROM
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						OR = {
							state = 605
							state = 753
							state = 823
							state = 748
						}
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.600.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.601 }
			remove_from_faction = ROOT
			end_puppet = ROOT
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.25
		add_war_support = -0.25
	}
}
